ON;`; await this.exec_sql(sql); // 如果所有表都删除失败，则抛出错误 if (errors.length === tns.length) { sql = `SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name NOT LIKE 'sqlite_%';`; const remaining_tables = await this.exec_sql(sql); throw new Error(`删除所有表失败：${JSON.stringify(errors)}，剩余表：${JSON.stringify(remaining_tables)}`); } // 如果有部分表删除失败，记录警告但不抛出错误 if (errors.length > 0) { result.results; } return result; } } return {_, DenoSqlite3, CloudflareD1}; })() function parseToUTC(time) { if (!time) return 0; if (time instanceof Date) return time.getTime(); if (typeof time === "number") return time; // 已经是时间戳 // 判断是否包含时区信息 // 带 Z 或 +HH:MM 或 -HH:MM 表示已经带时区 if (/[zZ]|[+-]\d{2}:\d{2}$/.test(time)) { return new Date(time).getTime(); } // 否则，假设是 MySQL DATETIME "YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss" 格式，手动解析为 UTC const [datePart, timePart] = time.split(" "); if (!datePart || !timePart) throw new Error("Invalid datetime format"); const [year, month, day] = datePart.split("-").map(Number); const [hour, minute, second] = timePart.split(":").map(Number); // Date.UTC 返回 UTC 毫秒时间戳 return Date.UTC(year, month - 1, day, hour, minute, second); } /* * 文件存储后端 * */ const filestorebackends = (() => { class _ { constructor(server) { this.server = server; this.prefix = filestorebackendargs.prefix; } async init() { throw new Error("虚函数"); } async put(key, value) { throw new Error("虚函数"); // boolean } async get(key) { throw new Error("虚函数"); // Uint8Array } async remove(key) { throw new Error("虚函数"); // boolean } } class DenoFile extends _ { constructor(server) { super(server); value) { key = `${this.prefix}-${key}`; await Deno.writeFile(`${this.saveto}/${key}`, new Uint8Array(value), {mode: 0o777}); return true; } async get(key) { key = `${this.prefix}-${key}`; return await // 用户注册 static async register(args) { if (this.server.req.method !== "POST") { return responsetypes.code_405(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "Method Not Allowed"})); } let d = await this.server.req.json(); // 参数白名单验证 - 防止权限注入攻击 const allowed_fields = ["account", "password", "invite_code"]; const request_fields = Object.keys(d); // 检查是否存在白名单之外的额外字段 for (const field of request_fields) { if (!allowed_fields.includes(field)) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, JSON.stringify({ message: "请求包含非法字段", invalid_field: field })); } } const account = normalizeId(d.account); const password = d.password; const invite_code = d.invite_code; // 验证输入 if (!account || account.length === 0) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "账号不能为空"})); } if (!password || password.length === 0) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "密码不能为空"})); } if (!invite_code || invite_code.length === 0) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "邀请码不能为空"})); } // 验证邀请码（仅检查邀请码是否存在，不检查使用状态，允许复用） let sql = `SELECT * FROM "invitation_code" WHERE "code" = ?;`; const invite_codes = await this.server.databasebackend.exec_sql(sql, [invite_code]); if (!invite_codes || invite_codes.length === 0) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "邀请码无效"})); } // 检查账号是否已存在 let existing_user = await this.server.databasebackend.user__get_attr(account); if (existing_user) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "账号已存在"})); } // 生成密码哈希（使用SHA-256） const encoder = new TextEncoder(); const data = encoder.encode(password); const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data); const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer)); const password_hash = hashArray.map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join(''); // 创建用户 const user_attr = { uid: account, password_hash: password_hash, disabled: false, // 停用 name: "", // 名称 free_space: 5120, // 储存空间 5120mb groups: [], // 所属组 contact_any: false, // 允许主动与所有用户通信 contact_groups: [], // 允许主动与这些组通信 contact_users: [], // 允许主动与这些用户通信 manage_drive: false, // 允许管理所有用户的网盘 }; const result = await this.server.databasebackend.user__new(user_attr); if (!result) { return responsetypes.code_500(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "注册失败"})); } // 邀请码不标记为已使用，允许复用 return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify({ success: true, message: "注册成功" })); } } class Admin extends _ { constructor(server) return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify(result)); } } static ws_action_type = { // api/* sync: 1, sync_one: 2, act: 3, send: 4, // load: 5, load_history: 6, read: 7, edit: 8, revoke: 9, sync_message: 10, mark_read: 11, clear: 12, forward: 13, } static async _ws_open__deno(args) { const {socket, response} = Deno.upgradeWebSocket(this.server.req); socket.onopen = (event) => { // console.log("websocket 已连接", event); }; socket.onmessage = async (event) => { const json = await subviews.Chat._ws_receive.call(this, args, event.data); socket.send(JSON.stringify(json)); }; socket.onclose = (event) => { // console.log("websocket 已关闭", event); }; socket.onerror = (event) => { // console.log("websocket 发送错误", event); }; return response; } static async _ws_open__cloudflare(args) { const [client, server] = Object.values(new WebSocketPair()); server.accept(); // 请求并发控制 let pendingCount = 0; const maxPending = 3; // 最大并发请求数，避免超过 Cloudflare Workers 子请求限制 server.addEventListener("message", async (event) => { // 先解析 JSON 获取 counter let json; try { json = JSON.parse(event.data); } catch (err) { server.send(JSON.stringify({ error: { name: err.name, message: err.message } })); return; } // 检查并发限制 if (pendingCount >= maxPending) { server.send(JSON.stringify({ counter: json.counter, error: { name: "Error", message: "Too many concurrent requests, please retry later" } })); return; } pendingCount++; try { const result = await subviews.Chat._ws_receive.call(this, args, event.data); server.send(JSON.stringify(result)); } catch (err) { server.send(JSON.stringify({ counter: json.counter, error: { name: err.name, message: err.message } })); } finally { pendingCount--; } }); server.addEventListener("close", (event) => { // console.log("websocket 已关闭", event); }); return responsetypes.code_101(this.server, null, {}, {webSocket: client,}); } static async _ws_receive(args, data) { // console.log("websocket 收到消息", data); const resp = {} let json; try { json = JSON.parse(data); } catch (err) { resp.error = {name: err.name, message: err.message, stack: err.stack, payload: err.payload,} return resp; } resp.action = json.action; resp.counter = json.counter; // 预先获取并缓存 user_attr，避免每个 action 重复查询 try { this._cached_user_attr = await this.server.databasebackend.user__get_attr_by_id( this.server.session_attr.user_id ); } catch (err) { resp.error = {name: err.name, message: err.message, stack: err.stack, payload: err.payload,} return resp; } // 处理动作 try { if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.sync) { resp.result = await Chat._action__sync.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.sync_one) { resp.result = await Chat._action__sync_one.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.act) { resp.result = await Chat._action__act.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.send) { resp.result = await Chat._action__send.call(this, json, undefined); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.load) { resp.result = await Chat._action__load.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.load_history) { resp.result = await Chat._action__load_history.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.read) { resp.result = await Chat._action__read.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.edit) { resp.result = await Chat._action__edit.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.revoke) { resp.result = await Chat._action__revoke.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.sync_message) { resp.result = await Chat._action__sync_message.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.mark_read) { resp.result = await Chat._action__mark_read.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.clear) { resp.result = await Chat._action__clear.call(this, json); } // else if (json.action === subviews.Chat.ws_action_type.forward) { resp.result = await Chat._action__forward.call(this, json); } // } catch (err) { resp.error = {name: err.name, message: err.message, stack: err.stack, payload: err.payload,} } finally { this._cached_user_attr = null; // 清理缓存 } return resp; } static async ws(args) { if (this.server.req.method === requestmethodtypes.GET) { if (this.server.req.headers.get("upgrade")?.toLowerCase() !== "websocket") return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, "不是Websocket。"); if (isPlatform(Platforms.deno)) { return await subviews.Chat._ws_open__deno.call(this, args); } else if (isPlatform(Platforms.cloudflare)) { return await subviews.Chat._ws_open__cloudflare.call(this, args); } else { return responsetypes.code_500(this.server, "平台不支持Websocket。"); } } } // 候选词 API 接口 static async candidates(args) { if (this.server.req.method === requestmethodtypes.GET) { // 获取筛选参数 const filter = this.server.requrl.searchParams.get("filter") || ""; } // 返回加密数据给前端，由前端负责解密 return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify({ success: true, encrypted: true, data: phrases_setting.encrypted_value })); } } // 群公告 API 接口 static async get_announcement(args) { if (this.server.req.method === requestmethodtypes.GET) { const gid = this.server.requrl.searchParams.get("gid"); const {user_ids} = r; if (!user_ids || !Array.isArray(user_ids) || user_ids.length === 0) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, requsterror.format_param("user_ids")); } // 批量获取用户信息 const users = {}; for (const user_id of user_ids) { const user_attr = await this.server.databasebackend.user__get_attr_by_id(user_id); if (user_attr) { users[user_id] = { id: user_attr.id, name: user_attr.name, email: user_attr.email }; } } return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify({ users: users })); } } // ========================================== // 修改个人聊天名称专属接口 // ========================================== static async rename_my_uid(args) { if (this.server.req.method === requestmethodtypes.POST) { const r = await this.server.req.json(); if (check_exist && check_exist.length > 0) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, "⚠️ 该名称已被别人占用，请换一个更酷的名字吧！"); } // 更新用户名称 await this.server.databasebackend.exec_sql(`UPDATE "user" SET uid = ? WHERE id = ?`, [new_uid, my_id]); return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify({success: true, message: `🎉 成功将聊天名称修改为【${new_uid}】！`})); } } // ========================================== // 社交功能 API 接口 // ========================================== // 添加好友接口 static async add_friend(args) { if (this.server.req.method === requestmethodtypes.POST) { const r = await this.server.req.json(); const target_uid = normalizeId(r.target_uid); const my_id = this.server.session_attr.user_id; // 获取当前用户信息 const my_attr = await this.server.databasebackend.user__get_attr_by_id(my_id); if (!my_attr) { return responsetypes.code_401(this.server, "未登录"); } // 检查权许 if (!my_attr.can_add_friend) { return responsetypes.code_403(this.server, "您没有添加好友的权限"); } // 获取目标用户信息 const target_attr = await this.server.databasebackend.user__get_attr(target_uid); if (!target_attr) { return responsetypes.code_404(this.server, "找不到该用户，请检查用户名"); } // 防止自己添加自己 if (my_id === target_attr.id) { return responsetypes.code_400(this.server, "不能添加自己为好友"); } // 双向添加好友关系（使用 ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING 防止重复添加） let sql1 = `INSERT INTO "user_contact_user_set" ("user_id", "other_user_id") VALUES (?, ?) ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING;`; await this.server.databasebackend.exec_sql(sql2, [target_attr.id, my_id]); return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify({success: true, message: "添加好友成功！"}), {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}); AND group_id = ?`, [my_id, group_attr.id] ); if (check_my_membership.length === 0) { return responsetypes.code_403(this.server, "你不是该群组成员，无法拉人"); } // 检查要邀请的目标用户是否存在 let target_attr = await this.server.databasebackend.user__get_attr(target_uid); if (!target_attr) { return responsetypes.code_404(this.server, "找不到要邀请的用户，请检查用户名"); } // 将目标用户拉入群组（使用 ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING 防止重复拉入报错） let sql = `INSERT INTO "user_group_set" ("user_id", "group_id") VALUES (?, ?) ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING;`; await this.server.databasebackend.exec_sql(sql, [target_attr.id, group_attr.id]); return responsetypes.code_200(this.server, JSON.stringify({success: true, message: `成功将【${target_uid}】邀请进入群聊【${gid}】！`}), {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}); } // 处理非POST请求 return responsetypes.code_405(this.server, JSON.stringify({message: "Method Not Allowed"})); } } return
